**Triad Verdict**
All three reviewers converge on the same recommendation: do **not** land the current 3a+3b+3c bundle. Land Phase 3a as a clean subset first, then review/commit Phase 3b and Phase 3c separately.

The tree is not just failing because of `mutedSenders`. That is the first visible compile failure, but static review found additional Android compile breaks and a server/client API contract mismatch.

**Reviewer A: Server**
Green:
- Phase 3a server core is directionally sound: `renderer`, `template`, template schemas, DB columns, and 0006 migration exist.
- Backwards compatibility is mostly handled by defaulting `renderer` to `"script"` and conditionally omitting template fields from script publish envelopes.
- Phase 2 dismiss filtering carry-over is implemented in [messages.py](D:/Projects/syncler/server/app/services/messages.py:195).

Yellow:
- Phase 3a lacks dedicated tests for golden template publish, bad JSONPath, unknown layout, missing `title`, endpoint mismatch, duplicate action ids, and default script behavior.
- Template payload output length caps cannot be enforced server-side because payloads are encrypted; Android must cap rendered values.

Red:
- Phase 3b fields are accepted in schema but not signed, validated, persisted, or returned correctly.
- `/v1/cards/upsert` likely 500s because `decode_base64` is called with positional `field_name`.
- Phase 3b delete endpoint diverges from plan and is ambiguous across users.
- `/v1/messages/inbox` still returns `messages`, not merged `items`, so it does not satisfy Phase 3b and disagrees with Android.
- Live-card upsert does not reject revoked plugins and trusts caller-provided `expires_at` instead of server-setting 48h TTL.

Prescription:
1. For Phase 3a clean landing, quarantine Phase 3b server exposure: defer `cards` router/0007/live-card public contract or finish all 3b properly.
2. Add Phase 3a server tests.
3. Keep 0006, renderer/template model/schema/router/service flow, SDK publishing support, and dismiss filtering.

**Reviewer B: Android Inbox / Template**
Green:
- Phase 3a DTOs and renderer intent exist.
- Dismiss refresh handling is present.
- Phase 3b UI intent is sketched, but incomplete.

Red:
- `TemplateCard` declaration and call site do not match: [TemplateCard.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/inbox/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/inbox/TemplateCard.kt:56) vs [InboxScreen.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/inbox/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/inbox/InboxScreen.kt:944).
- `TemplateCard` calls `runTemplateAction(action, payloadJson)`, but the VM takes `(String, String, String)`.
- [InboxRepository.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/inbox/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/inbox/InboxRepository.kt:94) calls missing `decryptLiveCard` / `decryptEventMessage`.
- [InboxRepository.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/inbox/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/inbox/InboxRepository.kt:166) references `InboxFeedItemDto` without importing it.
- [InboxScreen.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/feature/inbox/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/feature/inbox/InboxScreen.kt:230) calls missing `repository.revokeSender`.
- Android expects `/v1/messages/inbox` to return `items`, but server returns `messages`.

Prescription:
1. Freeze Phase 3b Android until 3a compiles, or finish 3b end-to-end. Smallest 3a path is to restore event-message inbox DTO handling.
2. Make `TemplateCard` stateless: accept `modifier` and `onAction(id, endpoint)`, remove `hiltViewModel()` from the composable.
3. Add rendered payload caps matching `hostPreview`.
4. Add focused tests for JSONPath, action callback, caps, script fallback, and dismiss refresh.

**Reviewer C: Storage / Settings**
Green:
- `MuteStore` effective mute formula matches the Phase 3c plan: synced mutes plus local mutes minus local unmutes.
- Inbox filtering already consumes `mutedSenderIds`.

Red:
- Build root cause: [MuteStore.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/core/storage/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/storage/MuteStore.kt:57) references `EncryptedUserState.mutedSenders`, but [EncryptedUserState.kt](D:/Projects/syncler/android/core/storage/src/main/kotlin/app/syncler/core/storage/EncryptedUserState.kt:13) has no field, JSON serialization, parser, or merger support.
- The plan’s `Set<String>` plus union semantics cannot reliably support “unmute everywhere” under stale/offline merge. Union resurrects removed values.

Prescription:
1. Minimum compile unblock: add `mutedSenders: Set<String> = emptySet()` to `EncryptedUserState`, serialize/parse `muted_senders`, and include it in `StateMerger`.
2. If Phase 3c lands after V4 as a separate commit, bump to V5. If it lands in the same schema wave as V4, keeping V4 is defensible per the plan.
3. Decide semantics before real Phase 3c landing: either accept monotonic union mutes, or use LWW/tombstone metadata for reliable unmute.
4. Add storage tests before UI polish.

**My Overall Recommendation**
The repair sequence should be:

1. Restore a green Phase 3a-only surface:
   - Keep renderer/template server + SDK + Android template dispatch.
   - Keep server dismiss filtering.
   - Remove or quarantine incomplete 3b/3c compile paths from the Phase 3a commit.

2. Fix Phase 3a Android compile issues:
   - Align `TemplateCard` API with `InboxScreen`.
   - Restore current server inbox DTO contract unless Phase 3b is completed immediately.
   - Avoid `MuteStore` and settings sheet in the Phase 3a commit.

3. Add Phase 3a tests, then commit Phase 3a.

4. Reintroduce Phase 3b as a coherent server/client contract change:
   - signed/stored/returned `card_type` and `card_key_path`;
   - `/v1/messages/inbox` feed response with `items`;
   - live decrypt/AAD/sequence gate;
   - delete/upsert/TTL/rate-limit tests.

5. Reintroduce Phase 3c after deciding synced mute merge semantics.
